****** Response Body For Transaction With Id 1552 ******
var down = true;
function showHelp(){
	down=!down;
	if (down){
		document.getElementById("HELP_DOWN").style.display = "inline";
		document.getElementById("HELP_UP").style.display   = "none";		
		document.getElementById("HELP_BOX").style.display  = "none";
	}else{	
		document.getElementById("HELP_DOWN").style.display = "none";
		document.getElementById("HELP_UP").style.display   = "inline";		
		document.getElementById("HELP_BOX").style.display  = "block";
	}	
}
